Met 1/2 n/p: Method: Using trigonometric identities

2. So I = Int[-1/2*cos(2*(4*x + 1)) + 1/4*cos(4*(4*x + 1)) + 1/4] dx
3. Integrate each term separately.
4. Int[-1/2*cos(2*(4*x + 1))] dx = -1/16*sin(2*(4*x + 1))

6. Int[1/4] dx = 1/4*x

8. Simplify.

231. [Integrate] Random integrate sub 796: sqrt [format fuzz] [integrate_sub:sqrt]
================================================================================

1
(1) *(sqrt(1x  -7))
4
1  * x-7

Check:
check; calculated answer correctness; random input formatting fuzzed

Output:
1 int
2 de
3 param area
M: f: 1 auto
2 dir
3 trig
4 sub
Met 1/2 n/p: u: Method: Integration by substitution
1. u = x - 7
2. du/dx = 1
3. du = dx
4. I = Int[sqrt(u)] du
5. = 2/3*u^(3/2) + C
6. Substitute back u = x - 7.
7. = 2/3*(x - 7)^(3/2) + C

7. Int[1/16*cos(8*(6*x - 1/4*pi))] dx = 1/768*sin(8*(6*x - 1/4*pi))
8. Int[1/16] dx = 1/16*x
9. = -1/48*sin(2*(6*x - 1/4*pi)) + 1/64*sin(4*(6*x - 1/4*pi)) - 1/144*sin(6*(6*x - 1/4*pi)) + 1/768*sin(8*(6*x - 1/4*pi)) + 1/16*x + C

2 de
3 param area
M: f: 1 auto
2 dir
3 trig
4 sub

8. Int[1/16] dx = 1/16*x
9. = -1/40*sin(2*(5*x + 1/6*pi)) + 3/160*sin(4*(5*x + 1/6*pi)) - 1/120*sin(6*(5*x + 1/6*pi)) + 1/640*sin(8*(5*x + 1/6*pi)) + 1/16*x + C
10. Simplify.
= -1/40*sin(10*x + 1/3*pi) + 3/160*sin(20*x + 2/3*pi) - 1/120*sin(30*x + pi) + 1/640*sin(40*x + 4/3*pi) + 1/16*x + C
